	{
		var groupIdsObj = {};
		Target2sell.basketProductGroupIds().split('|').forEach(function (gId) {
			groupIdsObj[gId] = gId;
		});
		
		var qtyObj = {};//{pid: qty}
		TMPCounter.basket.forEach(function (item)
		{
			if (groupIdsObj.hasOwnProperty(item['pid']))
			{
				if (!qtyObj.hasOwnProperty(item['pid']))
					qtyObj[item['pid']] = 0;
				
				qtyObj[item['pid']] = parseInt(qtyObj[item['pid']], 10) + parseInt(item['qty'], 10);
			}
		});
		
		var qty = [];
		for (var p in qtyObj)
		{
			qty.push(qtyObj[p]);
		}
		
		return qty.join('|');
	};
	Target2sell.wishList = function ()
	{
		if (!this.memorize['wish_list'])
			this.memorize['wish_list'] = TMPCounter.wish_list.join("|");
		
		return this.memorize['wish_list'];
	};
	Target2sell.basketProductGroupIds = function ()
	{
		var productGroupIdsObj = {};
		TMPCounter.basket.forEach(function (item)
		{
			if (item['pid'])
			{
				productGroupIdsObj[item['pid']] = item['pid'];
			}
		});
		
		return Object.keys(productGroupIdsObj).join('|');
	};
}catch(err){}
//-->
  </script>
